ef_on_monthly_pulse_recurence = {
	update_modifiers_bc_fc_ns = yes 
	com_topbar_save_game_compatibility_EF = yes #à sup dans quelque mois

	if  = {
		limit = {
			market_owner_is_root = yes 
			or = {
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes 
				market_owner_is_root_with_buiding_subject_building_modifier = yes
			}
		}
		remove_suject_currency = yes
		#les pays issu d'une sphere d'influence déclanchera automatiquement une crise de la devise quand il s'arrete
	}
	if  = {
		limit = {
			market_owner_is_root = no
			or = {
				market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no
				not_the_same_monetary_system_as_overlord = yes
				subjetc_no_modifier_on_bc = yes
			}
		}
		subject_currency = yes
		central_bank_production_methods = yes
	}

	#for new country by revolution
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_revolutionary = yes
			not  = {
				has_variable = coal_release_quantity
			}
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = for_new_country_je_2
		}
	}
}

	############################################################################################################################################################

	currency_strength_modifier = yes
	government_loan_month = yes
	building_ef_private_construction_modifier = yes

	#inflation_value & modifier -> interet si possede une devise sinon non
	inflation_modifier = yes
	inflation_on_consumer_goods_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	inflation_on_energy_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	inflation_on_raw_material_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	inflation_on_manufactured_goods_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	inflation_on_military_equipment_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	money_value_dif_01_market_value_fluctuations = yes

	every_country = {
		limit = {
			global_country_ranking = 1
		} 
		global_gold_silver_production = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					global_var:money_value_median = 0
					global_var:money_value_median = 1
				}
			}
			currency_law_list = yes
			money_value_global_var = yes
			median_currency_value = yes
		}
	}

	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		global_monetary_reference_global_var_fixe = yes
	}

	#monetary_policy_player
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_system
				has_law = law_type:law_fiat_standard
			}
			not = {
				has_law = law_type:law_isolationism
				or  = {
					var:currency_crisis >= 1
					var:central_bank_bankruptcy >= 1 #temps de que le pays reset en, extreme weajk currency cela va va déclanvher la crise -> une crise ce déckanche dure 2 ans si à l'issu des 2ans le pays est toujour en extreme weak currency il va retrigger la crise
					var:extreme_weak_currency_solution_count > 1
				}
			}
			#ajout d'une condition pour  les pays qui passe en law_fiat_standard par la crise quand sera intégré
		}
		activate_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		central_bank_production_methods = yes
	}

	#has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_system
	#has_law = law_type:law_fiat_standard

	#activate_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_system
	#activate_law = law_type:law_fiat_standard
	#activate_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
	#activate_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
	#activate_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
	#activate_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard

	#monetary_policy_player
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					not = {
						has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
					}
					var:devaluation_on = 1
					var:revaluation_on = 1
				}
			}
			monetary_policy_inflation = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
				or = {
					var:monetary_policy_inflation > 0
					var:monetary_policy_inflation < 0
				}
			}
			monetary_policy_inflation_reset = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				market_owner_is_root_4 = no
				or = {
					has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_25
					has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_50
					has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_75
					has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_100
					has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_25
					has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_50
					has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_75
					has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_100
				}
			}
			monetary_policy_inflation_reset_law = yes

		}
	}

	#stockpiling_currency_and_gold -> à décompposé je pense
	if  = {
		limit = {
			market_owner_is_root  = yes

			#-> à décompposé je pense
			#-> à voirr si on veux que la balance de commerce existe pour le joueur runiquement meme avec un pays sans dezvise il va faloirr décomposé

			# not  = {
			# 	is_subject_custom_trigger = yes # -> Criticable car il existe des sujet qui  possede leurr proprre marché donc non
			# }
		}
		stockpiling_central_bank_metal_reserves_state = yes 
		stockpiling_currency = yes
		trade_balance = yes #test 1mois
	}

	if  = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = foreign_exchange_controls
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				var:devaluation_on = 1
			}
			devaluation_on = yes
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				var:revaluation_on = 1
			}
			revaluation_on = yes
		}
	}
}

			# 	has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
			# 	has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			# }
		}
		ai_credit_at_central_bank = yes
		ai_refund_central_bank = yes
		ai_currency_deflation_inflation = yes
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
		}
		reference_currency_in_gold_fixe = yes
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			offshore_port_num > 0
		}
		is_treaty_port_disable_pm_market_liquidity = yes
	} 
	crisis_general_reset_count = yes
}

ef_on_yearly_pulse_reset = {

	#sell_limit_var_0
	if  = {
		limit = {
			not = {
				var:sell_limit_var_1 = 0 #?
			}
		}
		#sell_limit_var_0 = yes
		set_variable = {
			name = sell_limit_var_1
			value = 0
		}
	}

	#forex limite
	if  = {
		limit = {
			not = {
				var:sell_limit_currency_var_1 = 0 #?
			}
		}
		#sell_limit_currency_var_0 = yes
		set_variable = {
			name = sell_limit_currency_var_1
			value = 0
		}
	}

	#looting_1_year
	if  = {
		limit = {
			var:looting_1_year = 1
		}
		looting_1_year_on_action = yes
	}

	#goods_contract
	if  = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}

		#grain
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:grain_contract_1_year = 1
			}
			clear_grain_contract_1_year = yes
		}
		#wood

			}

central_bank_ef_on_yearly_pulse_country = {

	####
	#test
	#central_bank_interest -> pour que l'on prete à un sujet il ne peut pas etre un sujet et doit avoir GS ou GES
	central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes
	####

	if  = {
		limit  = {
			or  = {
				has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes
			}
		}
		cumulative_inflation_5_year = yes
		cumulative_inflation_10_year = yes
		cumulative_inflation_since_beginning = yes
		fluctuations_money_value_5_year = yes
		fluctuations_money_value_10_year = yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			is_ai = yes
			market_owner_is_root = yes
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_NISO = yes #No GES
		}
		ai_buy_sell_currency = yes
		monetary_systeme_transition = yes
	}

	#credit_at_central
	if = {
		limit = {
			credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_month > 5
			or  = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			}
		}
		credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_week = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = interest_at_the_central_bank
			credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_month < 5
			or  = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			}
		}
		credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_week_off = yes
	}

	#production_methods
	investement_pool_borrowing = yes
	central_bank_production_methods = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			market_owner_is_root = no
			market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = no #na pas la configuration deja sujet actif evite les répétition
		}
		central_bank_production_methods_2 = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			#securisé avec un trigger qui est invalide si la pm no subjet currency est selectionné
		}
		central_bank_production_methods_3 = yes
	}

	#money_value_target for ssubjectt or 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_ai = yes
			or  = {
				is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
				var:money_value_target_1 = 0
			}
		}
		money_value_target_modification = yes
	} 
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_ai = yes
			is_extreme_weak_currency = yes
			is_revolutionary = no
			not = {
				has_law = law_type:law_isolationism #extreme_weak_currency est normal
			}
		}
		extreme_weak_currency_solution = yes
	}
	
	#is_extreme_weak_currency_solution_player
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_ai = no
			is_extreme_weak_currency = yes
			is_revolutionary = no
			not = {
				has_law = law_type:law_isolationism #extreme_weak_currency est normal
			}
		}
		extreme_weak_currency_solution_player = yes
	} 

	establish_bank_compagnie = yes

	economic_instability_count_reset_condition = yes  

	currency_crisis_count_reset_condition = yes
	central_bank_bankruptcy_count_reset_condition = yes
	economic_crisis_count_reset_condition = yes
}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
			is_ai = yes
			not  = {
				is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		money_value_target_modification = yes 
	}
}
fiancial_center_ef_on_five_year_pulse_country = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = has_financial_center
			not  = {
				is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		position_regulator = yes
	}
}

ai_buy_sell_currency = {
	#begin_tag_3
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			money_value_dinar > 0
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				not = {
					or   = {
						is_weak_currency = yes
						is_extreme_weak_currency = yes
					}
				}
			}
			buy_dinar_currency = yes
		}
		if  = {
			limit  = {
				stockpiling_dinar_state > 1000000
				var:purchase_cycle = 0
			}
			sell_dinar_currency = yes
		}
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			money_value_dinar_algerian_dinar > 0
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				not = {
					or   = {
						is_weak_currency = yes
						is_extreme_weak_currency = yes
					}
				}
			}
			buy_dinar_algerian_dinar_currency = yes
		}
		if  = {
			limit  = {
				stockpiling_dinar_algerian_dinar_state > 1000000
				var:purchase_cycle = 0
			}
			sell_dinar_algerian_dinar_currency = yes
		}
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			money_value_dinar_iraqi_dinar > 0
		}
		if  = {

				scope:target_country = {
					has_law = law_type:law_spe_zloti_currency
					or = {
							var:currency_crisis = 1
						var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
					}
				}
				stockpiling_spe_zloti_state > 0
			}
			sell_spe_zloti_currency_crisis = yes
		}
		#thaler_hannoveraner_thaler
		else_if  = {
			limit  = {
				scope:target_country = {
					has_law = law_type:law_thaler_hannoveraner_thaler_currency
					or = {
							var:currency_crisis = 1
						var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
					}
				}
				stockpiling_thaler_hannoveraner_thaler_state > 0
			}
			sell_thaler_hannoveraner_thaler_currency_crisis = yes
		}
		#thaler_prussian_thaler
		else_if  = {
			limit  = {
				scope:target_country = {
					has_law = law_type:law_thaler_prussian_thaler_currency
					or = {
							var:currency_crisis = 1
						var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
					}
				}
				stockpiling_thaler_prussian_thaler_state > 0
			}
			sell_thaler_prussian_thaler_currency_crisis = yes
		}
		#thaler_saxon_thaler
		else_if  = {
			limit  = {
				scope:target_country = {
					has_law = law_type:law_thaler_saxon_thaler_currency
					or = {
							var:currency_crisis = 1
						var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
					}
				}
				stockpiling_thaler_saxon_thaler_state > 0
			}
			sell_thaler_saxon_thaler_currency_crisis = yes
		}
	#brace

update_modifiers_bc_fc_ns = {
	#si il n'a pas le batiment il ne délanche pas
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_bank
			}
		}
		central_bank_modifier = yes
		stockpiling_capital_state_transfert = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				or = {
					has_building = building_financial_centre
					has_building = building_financial_centre_arg
					has_building = building_financial_centre_aus
					has_building = building_financial_centre_bav
					has_building = building_financial_centre_bel
					has_building = building_financial_centre_bic
					has_building = building_financial_centre_brz
					has_building = building_financial_centre_chi
					has_building = building_financial_centre_chl
					has_building = building_financial_centre_den
					has_building = building_financial_centre_dei
					has_building = building_financial_centre_egy
					has_building = building_financial_centre_fra
					has_building = building_financial_centre_frm
					has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr
					has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr_2
					has_building = building_financial_centre_gre
					has_building = building_financial_centre_hkh
					has_building = building_financial_centre_han
					has_building = building_financial_centre_ita
					has_building = building_financial_centre_jap
					has_building = building_financial_centre_mex
					has_building = building_financial_centre_net
					has_building = building_financial_centre_nsw
					has_building = building_financial_centre_ont
					has_building = building_financial_centre_peu
					has_building = building_financial_centre_por
					has_building = building_financial_centre_pru
					has_building = building_financial_centre_que
					has_building = building_financial_centre_rus
					has_building = building_financial_centre_saf
					has_building = building_financial_centre_sar
					has_building = building_financial_centre_sic
					has_building = building_financial_centre_spa
					has_building = building_financial_centre_swe
					has_building = building_financial_centre_swi
					has_building = building_financial_centre_tus
					has_building = building_financial_centre_tur
					has_building = building_financial_centre_uru
					has_building = building_financial_centre_usa
					has_building = building_financial_centre_usa_2
					has_building = building_financial_centre_sax
				}
			}
		}
		financial_center_modifier = yes

		stockpiling_capital_state_transfert = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}
		}
		national_stockpile_modifier = yes

		stockpiling_capital_state_transfert = yes
	}

	#si il n'a pas ou si il a. il déclanche
	#remove_state_building_modifier = yes
	remove_country_building_modifier = yes
	destroy_building_not_allowed = yes

	if  = {  #réinitialis la loi si un pays si lib
		limit = {
			law_currency_enacted = yes
			not  = {
				country_already_central_bank = yes
			}
		}
		remove_law_currency = yes
	}

crisis_general_reset_count = {
	if = {
		limit  = { 
			var:economic_instability_count_count >= 1
			var:economic_instability_count = 0 
			is_at_war = no
		}  
		set_variable = {
			name = economic_instability_count_count
			value = 0
		}
	} 
	if = {
		limit  = { 
			var:central_bank_bankruptcy_count >= 1
			var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 0 
			is_at_war = no
		}  
		set_variable = {
			name = central_bank_bankruptcy_count
			value = 0
		}
	} 
	if = {
		limit  = { 
			var:currency_crisis_count >= 1
			var:currency_crisis = 0 
			is_at_war = no
		}  
		set_variable = {
			name = currency_crisis_count
			value = 0
		}
	} 
	if = {
		limit  = { 
			var:financial_crash_count >= 1
			var:financial_crash = 0 
			is_at_war = no
		}  
		set_variable = {
			name = financial_crash_count
			value = 0
		}
	} 
	if = {
		limit = { 
			var:economic_crisis_count >= 1
			var:economic_crisis = 0 
			is_at_war = no
		}  
		set_variable = {
			name = economic_crisis_count
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
#economic_instability
economic_instability_count_reset_condition = { 
	if = {
		limit  = { 
			var:economic_instability_count >= 1
			is_at_war = no
			not = {
				or = {
					has_modifier = economic_instability_country
					has_modifier = currency_crisis_country
					has_modifier = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
					has_modifier = financial_crash_country
					has_modifier = economic_crisis_country 
					has_modifier = declared_bankruptcy
				} 
			}
		} 
		economic_instability_count_reset = yes
	}
}

#economic_instability
economic_instability_count_reset = {
	change_variable = {
		name = economic_instability_count_count
		add = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit  = { 
			var:economic_instability_count_count >= 3
		} 

		set_variable = {
			name = economic_instability_count
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = economic_instability_count_count
			value = 0
		}
	}
} 
#central_bank_bankruptcy -> avec la nouvelle fonction de division par 2 central_bank_bankruptcy n'est plus direct et le pays peut assayer de ce rétablir
central_bank_bankruptcy_count_reset = {
	change_variable = {
		name = central_bank_bankruptcy_count
		add = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit  = { 
			var:central_bank_bankruptcy_count >= 3
		} 

		set_variable = {
			name = central_bank_bankruptcy
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = central_bank_bankruptcy_count
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
#currency_crisis
currency_crisis_count_reset = {
	change_variable = {
		name = currency_crisis_count
		add = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit  = { 
			var:currency_crisis_count >= 3
		} 

		set_variable = {
			name = currency_crisis
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = currency_crisis_count
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
